395        1/1              chksum_c0_w0_prev <=  16'h0;
396        1/1              chksum_c0_w1_prev <=  16'h0; 
397        1/1              chksum_c1_w0_prev <=  16'h0;
398        1/1              chksum_c1_w1_prev <=  16'h0;   
399        1/1            end else if (pre_chksum_en & bitstream_wack_o==1'b1 & ~cfg_done_o) begin
400        1/1              chksum_c0_w1_prev <=  chksum_c0_w1;
401        1/1              chksum_c1_w1_prev <=  chksum_c1_w1;
402        1/1              chksum_c0_w0_prev <=  chksum_c0_w0;
403        1/1              chksum_c1_w0_prev <=  chksum_c1_w0;
404        1/1            end else if (post_chksum_en & bitstream_rack_o==1'b1 & ~cfg_done_o) begin
405        1/1              chksum_c0_w1_prev <=  chksum_c0_w1;
406        1/1              chksum_c1_w1_prev <=  chksum_c1_w1;
407        1/1              chksum_c0_w0_prev <=  chksum_c0_w0;
408        1/1              chksum_c1_w0_prev <=  chksum_c1_w0;    
409                       end
                        MISSING_ELSE
410                     end
411                     
412                     
413                     // cfg done 
414                     wire chksum_status_w;
415                     
416                     assign chksum_status_w = ~(|(csum_w0 + chksum_c0_w1_prev + chksum_c1_w1_prev) || |(csum_w1 - chksum_c1_w1_prev)); 
417                     
418                     always_ff @(posedge clk, negedge rst_n)
419        2/2              if (!rst_n)                                            chksum_status_o <= 1'b0;
420        2/2              else if ( pre_chksum_en & kickoff_i & chksum_status_w) chksum_status_o <= 1'b1;
421        2/2              else if ( post_chksum_en & rx_proc  & chksum_status_w) chksum_status_o <= 1'b1;
422        2/2              else if (clr_kickoff_ff[2] )                           chksum_status_o <= 1'b0;
                        MISSING_ELSE
423                     
424                     always_ff @(posedge clk, negedge rst_n)
425        2/2              if (!rst_n)                                                cfg_done_o <= 1'b0;
426        2/2              else if (!pre_chksum_en & clr_kickoff_o)                   cfg_done_o <= 1'b1; 
427        2/2              else if ( pre_chksum_en & clr_kickoff_o & chksum_status_o) cfg_done_o <= 1'b1; 
428        1/1              else                                                       cfg_done_o <= 1'b0;
429                     
430                     
431                     ///////////////////////////////////
432                     
433                     assign shift_count_o = bitstream_bit_cnt[29:0];
434                     assign fsm_state_o = cfg_write_cur_st;
435                     
436                     ///////////////////////////////////
437                     
438                     logic ser_data;
439                     assign clk_in = ccff_clk_i[current_chain_num];
440                     
441                     assign en_clk = cfg_write_cur_st==SHIFT & !swith_chain_pause;
442                     
443                     clkgate ccff_clkgate (.clk(clk), .testmode(testmode), .clk_en(en_clk), .clk_out(clk_out), .clk_ooc());
444                     
445                     assign ser_data = shift_reg[0];
446
